***захватывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захватывать.html>захва́тывать</a> (6107)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватывать.html>захва́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxvátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grasp, to grip, to grab, to clench, to collar</li>
<li>to seize, to capture, to occupy, to usurp</li>
<li>to absorb, to captivate, to possess, to carry away, to thrill, to engross, to enthral</li>
<li>to catch, to snatch, to take (away)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take along
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зонт.html>зонт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чай</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождя́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Zaxvatí</b> zont na slúčaj doždjá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Grab</b> an umbrella in case of a rain.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захват.html>захва́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaxvát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватчик.html>захва́тчик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaxvátčik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">захва́тчица</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaxvátčica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захворать.html>захвора́ть</a> (22943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хворать.html>хвора́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvorátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захворать.html>захвора́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxvorátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хворать.html>хвора́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become sick, to fall ill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contract, to come down with <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an illness; + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***захлестнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захлестнуть.html>захлестну́ть</a> (13087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестнуть.html>хлестну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlestnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захлестнуть.html>захлестну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxlestnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захлестывать.html>захлёстывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flow over, to overflow <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a wave</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to lash <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">around</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:захлестнуть.html>захлестну́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тлей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaxlestnútʹ</b> kovó-libo pétlej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to catch smb in a noose; lasso smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веревка.html>верёвка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:захлестнуть.html>захлестну́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">verjóvka <b>zaxlestnúla</b> jevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the rope lashed round him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sweep over, to overwhelm</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlópatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захлопнуть.html>захло́пнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaxlópnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***захлопывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захлопывать.html>захло́пывать</a> (19397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захлопывать.html>захло́пывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxlópyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захлопнуть.html>захло́пнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slam, to bang (a door shut)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захлопывать.html>захло́пывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxlópyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захлопать.html>захло́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to interrupt with an applause</li></ol>

***захмелеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захмелеть.html>захмеле́ть</a> (15886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хмелеть.html>хмеле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xmelétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захмелеть.html>захмеле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxmelétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хмелеть.html>хмеле́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become intoxicated, to drunk, to tipsy or high</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become exhilarated</li></ol>

***заход.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заход.html>захо́д</a> (9751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заходить.html>заходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заход.html>захо́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заход.html>захо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заход.html>захо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заход.html>захо́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>recess, set, setting, sundown</li>
<li>stopping, calling <i>(a ship)</i>, approach <i>(an airplane)</i></li>
<li>attempt, trial</li>
<li>sunset
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заход.html>захо́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнца</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaxód</b> sólnca</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sunset</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> west
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запад.html>за́пад</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">západ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***заходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заходить.html>заходи́ть</a> (1306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заходить.html>заходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зайти.html>зайти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go (to see), to come in (to see, etc.), to call, to drop in</li>
<li>to pick up, to fetch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call at, to enter (a port)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to advance</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass, to draw out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to approach</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to outflank</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn, to disappear, to go behind</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> хе́льсинки <a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнце</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заходить.html>захо́дит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полночь.html>по́лночь</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V Xélʹsinki sólnce <b>zaxódit</b> v pólnočʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The sun <b>sets</b> at midnight in Helsinki.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***заходиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заходиться.html>заходи́ться</a> (22340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заходить.html>заходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заходиться.html>заходи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зайтись.html>зайти́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk oneself off one's feet (imperfective only)</li>
<li>to be beside oneself <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заходиться.html>заходи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:истерика.html>исте́рике</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaxodítʹsja</b> v istérike</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go hysterical</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заходиться.html>заходи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:истошный.html>исто́шном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>кри́ке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaxodítʹsja</b> v istóšnom kríke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scream one's head off; scream oneself into fits</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become/grow numb</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захолустье.html>захолу́стье</a> (26004)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захолустье.html>захолу́стье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxolústʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захолустье.html>захолу́стья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захолустье.html>захолу́стья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захолустье.html>захолу́стий</a></b>)
</p>
